RURAL DEVELOPMENT AND PANCHAYAT RAJ DEPARTMENT
DE-RESERVATION FOR THE OFFICES OF THE PRESIDENTS OF VILLAGE PANCHAYATS
UNDER THE TAMIL NADU PANCHAYATS ACT.
AMENDMENT TO NOTIFICATION
[G.O. Ms. No. 60, Rural Development and Panchayat Raj (PR-1) 9th September 2011,
ÝõE 23, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2042.]
No. II(2)/RDPR/396(g-1)/2011.
Under Section 57 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994) the Governor of
Tamil Nadu hereby makes the following amendment to the Rural Development and Panchayat Raj Department
Notification No.II(2)RDPR/453(f-1)/2006, published at pages 1 to 144 of Part II—Section 2 of the
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette Extraordinary, dated the 2nd September 2006, No. 228:
AMENDMENT
1. (a) In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the
District: Kancheepuram”, in the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “3. UTHIRAMERUR PANCHAYAT UNION”,
in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 1” in column (1) and “Pulipakkam” in column (2) thereof, for the expression,
“ST (General)”, the expression General” shall be substituted.
DTP—II-2 Ex. (318)—1


2
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
EX-II-2-318—F&U
(a) In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the District:
Kancheepuram”, in the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “11. CHITHAMUR PANCHAYAT UNION”,
in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 19” in column (1) and “Puthur” in column (2) thereof, for the expression, “SC (General)”,
the expression "General” shall be substituted.
2. In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the District: Thiruvallur”,
in the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “13. PALLIPET PANCHAYAT UNION”, in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 2”
in column (1) and “Ramapuram” in column (2) thereof, for the expression, “ST (General)”, the expression "General” shall be
substituted.
3. In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the District: Cuddalore”,
in the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “3. PANRUTI PANCHAYAT UNION”, in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 2”
in column (1) and “Kolapakkam” in column (2) thereof, for the expression, “SC (Women)”, the expression "General” shall be
substituted.
4. In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the District: Villupuram”,
in the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “13. VALLAM PANCHAYAT UNION”, in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 4”
in column (1) and “Kadugapattu” in column (2) thereof, for the expression, “SC (Women)”, the expression "General” shall be
substituted.
5. In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the District: Vellore”, in
the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “17. THIMIRI PANCHAYAT UNION”, in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 1”
in column (1) and “Seyyathuvannan” in column (2) thereof, for the expression, “ST (General)”, the expression "General” shall be
substituted.
6. In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the District: Thiruvannamalai”,
in the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “9. THANDARAMPET PANCHAYAT UNION”, in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 3”
in column (1) and “Perayampattu” in column (2) thereof, for the expression, “ST (General)”, the expression "General” shall be
substituted.
7. In the said Notification, under the heading “Reservation for Village Panchayat Presidents, Name of the District: Perambalur”,
in the Tabular column, under the sub-heading “9. T.PALUR  PANCHAYAT UNION”, in column (3), against the entry “Sl. No. 7”
in column (1) and “Naduvalur” in column (2) thereof, for the expression, “SC (General)”, the expression "General” shall be
substituted.
RESERVATION FOR THE OFFICES OF THE PRESIDENTS OF VILLAGE PANCHAYATS
[G.O. Ms. No. 61, Rural Development and Panchayat Raj (PR-1) 9th September 2011,
ÝõE 23, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2042.]
No. II(2)/RDPR/396(g-2)/2011.
Under Section 57 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994) the Governor of
Tamil Nadu reserves the offices of the Presidents of Village Panchayats for the persons belonging to Scheduled Castes/Scheduled
Tribes and for Women as indicated below:
The Presidents of Village Panchayats.
